<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intégrité</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">integrite</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">integritās</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:integer.html>integer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-iteit</i>.

***interessant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:interessant.html>interessant</a> (1120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intéressant</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intéresser</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:interessant.html>interessant</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:interessanter.html>interessanter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:interessantst.html>interessantst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:interesting.html>interesting</a>, arousing <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:holding.html>holding</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:attention.html>attention</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:fascinating.html>fascinating</a> <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 18th <a href = vnd.unilang:c.html>c</a>.]</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***intimidatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:intimidatie.html>intimidatie</a> (10457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:intimideren.html>intimideren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-atie</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intimidation</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*intimidatio</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">intimidare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> intimidate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:see.html>See</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">intimidate</i>.
